CREATE TABLE [dbo].[userTable] (
    [sid]      NVARCHAR (50) NOT NULL,
    [name]     NVARCHAR (50) NULL,
    [password] NVARCHAR (50) NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED ([sid] ASC)
);
Go

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[DelayTable] (
    [sid]        NVARCHAR(50)      NOT NULL,
    [name]       NVARCHAR (50)  NULL,
    [inschool]   NVARCHAR(50)           NULL,
    [birth]      NVARCHAR(50)           NULL,
    [housereg]   NVARCHAR (150) NULL,
    [college]    NVARCHAR (50)  NULL,
    [Department] NVARCHAR (50)  NULL,
    [schoolyear] NVARCHAR (50)   NULL,
    [semester]   NVARCHAR(50)      NULL,
    [prove]      NVARCHAR (150) NULL,
    CONSTRAINT [PK_DelayTable] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED ([sid] ASC)
);

GO

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[charstroke](
	[chword] [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	[stroke] [int] NULL
) ON [PRIMARY]

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[fiveelement](
	[elementname] [nchar](1) NOT NULL,
	[elementno] [int] NULL
) ON [PRIMARY]

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[namerule](
	[no] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
	[rule] [nvarchar](150) NULL,
	[result] [nvarchar](150) NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [PK_namerule] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[no] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]
GO
